Page 6

Britain and Italy Mutually Assure Each Other, No Hostility in Naval Activities

Easing of Tensions in Europe, Italian Prime Minister Raises Four Minimum Demands as Conditions for Solving East African Problem

(London) Britain has sought to ease tensions between Britain and Italy. The Foreign Office issued a statement today stating that Britain has no intention of attacking Italy, and detailing the mutual assurances exchanged between British Ambassador to Italy Drummond and Italian Deputy Foreign Minister Suvich in Rome. Ambassador Drummond stated that the movements and reinforcements of the British fleet to defend the Mediterranean were "a natural result of the recent fierce attacks on Britain by the Italian press." It is believed here that this statement by the Foreign Office is intended to make it easier for Italian Prime Minister Mussolini to adopt a more compromising attitude. As for Geneva, Mussolini's demands seem to be coming on strong, but the atmosphere has suddenly turned optimistic with the presentation of minimum conditions for abandoning war. The conditions proposed by Mussolini include the following three: (1) Italian Eritrea and Somalia must obtain territorial connections, with Abyssinia ceding a western region to Italy; (2) any sea route for Abyssinia must pass through a port in Italian territory; (3) the majority of the Abyssinian army must be dismissed and disarmed, with the remaining army under the control of Italian generals. It is understood that the League of Nations representatives are now following Britain's lead, and most do not believe that Britain can allow the expansion of the scope of the Five-Power Committee's recommendations, and expect that the League of Nations itself cannot accept these conditions, because accepting them would be tantamount to infringing on Abyssinia's sovereignty. (National News Agency dispatch, 22nd)

(London) British morning newspapers believe that the wording of the Italian government's announcement rejecting the Five-Member Special Committee's recommendations and its criticisms of the solution are a sign of improving situation. According to the Daily Telegraph, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini's minimum demands include the following four: (1) The area of land ceded to Italy must be more than that recommended; (2) Abyssinia's outlet to the sea must pass through Eritrea; (3) the Abyssinian army must be disarmed and reorganized by Italy; (4) sufficient land must be ceded to Italy so that Eritrea can be connected to Italian Somaliland. The Daily Telegraph advocates a policy of patience towards Italy, saying that the strong attitude taken by the League of Nations Council and the General Assembly has had a clear and powerful impression in Rome, and the concentration of the British Navy in the Mediterranean has made this impression even more profound. (Reuters dispatch, 23rd)

(Rome) Since Britain concentrated its navy in the Mediterranean, relations between Britain and Italy have been extremely tense. However, since Britain stated that its naval actions were unrelated to sanctions, people here have felt relieved, and the fear that the Italian-Abyssinian conflict could trigger a European war has also dissipated. At the same time, diplomatic negotiations between Britain, France, and Italy have resumed. If the League of Nations cannot resolve the difficult situation, it is hoped here that Britain, France, and Italy will hold another tripartite conference, at which Mussolini may personally attend. The attitude of the newspapers towards Britain is now becoming more moderate, and they are able to make more objective criticisms of the Five-Member Committee's recommendations. (National News Agency dispatch, 23rd)

Special Committee Meeting Yesterday After Receiving Italian and Abyssinian Replies

Recognizing Mediation Has Failed, Drafting Report to Submit to Executive Council

(Geneva) The Five-Power Committee met this morning and decided to continue deliberations tomorrow to draft a report to the League of Nations Executive Council on the failure of the Committee's mediation. According to political sources, the Committee believes that the reply from Mussolini delivered by Italian representative Aloisi cannot be accepted. According to Mussolini's demands, (1) Abyssinia must cede a strip of land so that Italian Eritrea and Somalia can be connected, and cede some land east of the Abyssinian capital to Italy; (2) in compensation for Abyssinia's territorial cession, Italy will provide a port in an Italian colony; (3) Abyssinia must completely disarm; (4) the police necessary for maintaining order must be controlled by Italy. (National News Agency dispatch, 23rd)

(Geneva) Italy firmly demands that land adjacent to Eritrea must be ceded to Italy and that Italy be granted a kind of jurisdiction over Abyssinia proper. The Italian-Abyssinian dispute is now gradually approaching a breaking point. It is generally believed that the situation is almost hopeless, and Italy may withdraw from the League of Nations. People here are now pessimistic, fearing that the Italian and Abyssinian views can never be reconciled. Italy's attitude against the proposals of the Five-Member Special Committee remains unchanged. According to today's news, Abyssinia has accepted the proposals of the Five-Member Special Committee, but with the proviso that its sovereignty must be preserved, the details of which are still to be discussed. French Prime Minister Laval arrived here from Paris this morning and immediately met with Italian representative Aloisi and Special Committee Chairman Madariaga. The Five-Member Special Committee meeting was held at 11 am, and it is said that Aloisi presented the Committee with Italy's formal response to the Committee's proposals. The meeting time was very short, only a few minutes, and then a public announcement was issued, stating that the Five-Member Special Committee met this morning to record Abyssinia's reply agreeing to the Committee's recommendations and to study Italy's reply with attached opinions. The Committee decided to report to the League of Nations Executive Council the general situation that can be seen from the official documents, etc. Chairman Madariaga will meet with representatives from both Italy and Abyssinia in the afternoon, and the Committee will hold another meeting tomorrow to draft a report to the League of Nations Executive Council, stating the course of the failed mediation. It is said that the Committee will study the articles of Article 15 of the League of Nations Covenant at tomorrow's meeting to serve as the basis for the League of Nations' future actions. (Reuters dispatch, 23rd)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Secretariat has just issued a bulletin stating that the Italian-Abyssinian Dispute Subcommittee held a meeting this morning to discuss Abyssinia's reply accepting the Committee's recommendations and the Italian government's answer, and decided to submit a report to the Executive Council to explain the situation. It is generally believed that the Committee decided to submit a report to the Executive Council because the replies from both Italy and Abyssinia have been received, and because the interests involved in the current dispute are extremely important, it is necessary to seek instructions from the Executive Council. French Prime Minister Laval met with Italian representative Aloisi before the Committee meeting, and British Minister of State Eden also discussed with Committee Chairman Madariaga. (Havas dispatch, 23rd)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Executive Council's Italian-Abyssinian Dispute Subcommittee is scheduled to hold a meeting tomorrow and prepare a report to be sent to the Executive Council. This report will include all relevant documents relating to the various negotiations conducted by the Committee since its establishment. It is generally expected that the Executive Council will hold a meeting tomorrow afternoon or the day after to discuss this report. (Havas dispatch, 23rd)

(Geneva) Observers believe that after Italy and Abyssinia responded to the Subcommittee, the situation of the Italian-Abyssinian dispute has reached its peak. Since the Abyssinian government has expressed its acceptance of the peace plan proposed by the Committee, Italy should be legally bound by Article 15, Paragraph 6 of the League of Nations Covenant and may not arbitrarily declare war on the country. However, judging from the demands made by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini yesterday, which almost amount to placing Abyssinia under Italian administration, they cannot be accepted by the League of Nations. On the British delegation's side, it is believed that the proposals made by the Subcommittee should be considered the maximum extent possible and that there is no possibility of further progress. This is because the recommendations can be said to have satisfied the requirements proposed by Italy. The Committee's advocacy of reorganizing the Abyssinian economic institutions is precisely to meet Italy's wishes. In addition, if this recommendation is submitted to the Executive Council for instructions, the Executive Council may not necessarily agree due to its own qualifications. Therefore, what Italy can obtain should be less than the Subcommittee's recommendations. (Havas dispatch, 23rd)

Italian Spokesperson Says Door to Reconciliation Not Closed, Awaiting New Proposals from League of Nations

(Rome) An authoritative spokesperson told a Reuters interviewer today that the door to reconciliation of the Italian-Abyssinian dispute remains open. Italy is currently awaiting new proposals from the League of Nations, and the minimum basis for discussion not included in the recent proposals of the Five-Power Committee may be seen in the new proposals. Italy has not submitted an answer. (Reuters dispatch, 23rd)

(Rome) It is claimed here that Italy will not withdraw from the League of Nations for the time being, and will only consider this when it is forced to do so. Italy's attitude, though not harmonious, is quite proper. It is noteworthy that the newspapers here have not recently advocated that Italy should withdraw from the League of Nations. (Reuters dispatch, 23rd)

(Rome) Foreign observers believe that the Italian people are currently calmly spending their daily lives, waiting for the development of the international situation regarding the Italian-Abyssinian dispute. There is no atmosphere of the eve of a great war here. The newspapers commented on the proposals of the League of Nations Executive Council Subcommittee, generally believing that although the Committee has recognized the necessity of reorganizing Abyssinian institutions, the proposed plan is limited to reorganizing the administrative institutions. However, if the reorganization of the administration does not have a solid foundation, in other words, if the entire Abyssinian nation is not thoroughly transformed, it is unlikely to succeed. (Havas dispatch, 23rd)

The Inside Story of Britain's Opposition to Italy's Use of Force in East Africa

Treating the Far East Route as a Lifeline, Not Upholding Justice for Small Nations

(New York) According to informed sources here, the real reason why Britain opposes Italian Prime Minister Mussolini's use of force against Abyssinia is not to protect justice for this small African country. The world generally believes that Europe is unlikely to have a war within ten years, but the current situation has changed. The British believe that Italy's current actions against Abyssinia are the vanguard of a colonial policy. If it succeeds, the status of all colonies in Africa will be threatened by Italy. If Britain's hegemony in the Mediterranean, Africa, and the Red Sea is seized by others, the foundation of the British Empire will shake, because the route from the Strait of Gibraltar through the Suez Canal, the Red Sea, to India, the Far East, Australia, and New Zealand is the lifeline of British commerce. The British people are firmly opposed to war, but defending their empire is another matter. Therefore, the British monarch can, in these times, transform from a passive position to become the leader of millions of loyal citizens of the country. If the cabinet decides that war is inevitable, the British monarch, although peace-loving, will also support its decision, and the entire nation will rise up to support the British monarch. Moreover, if Britain and Italy go to war, other countries will also be drawn into the vortex, because Britain and France are natural allies and have always jointly supported the League of Nations. France also has many allies on the continent. On the other hand, Italy is not isolated either. (National News Agency dispatch, 22nd)

British and Italian Navies Deploy in the Mediterranean

Mutual Assurance of Non-Aggression; British Ambassador Visits Mussolini

(London) The British and Italian governments have mutually assured each other that their naval activities in the Mediterranean are not for aggressive purposes. According to an official statement released by the British Foreign Office, on September 20th, the British Ambassador to Rome, Sir Eric Drummond, met with the Italian Undersecretary of State, Suvich, to inform him on behalf of the British government about the movements of the British fleet in the Mediterranean and the reinforcement of garrisons and war materials. He also stated that these British actions did not contain any intention of aggression and were solely a response to the anti-British campaign in the Italian press in recent weeks. Suvich replied that he was instructed to declare that Italy's military preparations in the Mediterranean were purely defensive and not intended for aggression. It is reported that Sir Eric Drummond's notification to the Italian government was not prompted by any formal protest from Rome but was initiated by the British government itself. (Reuters, 23rd)

(London) The purpose of the British Foreign Office's publication of the above communiqué is to alleviate the tension of the current situation, or perhaps to indicate that a conflict between Britain and Italy is not a real issue. Regarding this, officials have repeatedly stated that the British naval precautions have two objectives: first, to prepare Britain so that it can implement the provisions of the League of Nations Covenant once the League Council makes a decision; and second, to protect Britain's own interests in the event of an emergency. However, regardless of how circumstances change, Britain must consider the decisions of the League Council as a guide. As for the communiqué issued by the Italian Cabinet yesterday, officials have not commented on it, saying only that there is still hope for continued negotiations in Geneva. In short, officials hold an optimistic view of the situation and believe that the communiqué issued by the Foreign Office tonight should further smooth the way forward. (Havas, 22nd)

(London) The British Ambassador to Italy, Sir Eric Drummond, has recently received instructions from the government to meet with Italian Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Mussolini for talks. This move will have a significant impact on the development of the current situation. Since the recent dispute arose, Ambassador Drummond has only been in contact with Italian Undersecretary of State Suvich. Now that he is meeting with Prime Minister Mussolini, it will not be difficult to discern from their conversation whether Italy is seeking a political compromise on Abyssinia and whether the tense relationship between Britain and Italy can be eased. (Havas, 26th)

Gibraltar Port: The British troop transport ship "Naldera," carrying 1,600 infantry troops from Shorncliffe, arrived here this afternoon. Tomorrow, it will load munitions and sail to Malta. (Havas, 22nd)

(Tokyo) According to a telegram received by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the British government has announced that the British Navy in the Mediterranean consists of 144 ships, stationed as follows:

Alexandria: 28 ships; Aden: 10 ships; near Suez: 6 ships; Palestine: 20 ships; between Gibraltar and Malta: 70 ships. (Telecommunications, 23rd)

Italian Troops Continue to Deploy to East Africa

Naples: Italy is still sending troops to Africa. Last week, five transport ships, carrying over 6,000 soldiers and equipped with heavy vehicles, mules, artillery, and other war materials, departed for Africa. Among the officers was Captain Gillen, who is already sixty years old and participated in the Battle of Adowa (in which the Ethiopian army defeated the Italian army). He has volunteered to serve again. This week, another 3,000 people will depart for Africa. At the same time, troops from various parts of Italy continue to arrive here in a steady stream. The Governor of Rome, Bottai, is also one of the recent volunteers. He was received by Mussolini yesterday and will resign his post on the 28th to go on expedition. The Italian writer Gayda has also written an article published in a newspaper, saying that the plan formulated by the Committee of Five in Geneva does not involve the Abyssinian army. The Abyssinian army cannot be compared to the armies of other countries. Therefore, the Committee has not taken into account Italy's security. The tone of the article is much milder than his previous writings. (Reuters, 22nd)

Italian troops embarking for East Africa were inspected and discovered to be the private property of the Abyssinian ambassador to Britain.

(London) Regarding the claim by New York financier Chochik that he has obtained a concession in Abyssinia, it has now been clarified that the so-called concession was not granted by the Abyssinian government but is a private matter between Chochik and the Abyssinian Ambassador to Britain, Dr. Martin. Abyssinian King Inspects Air Force

Initiator of the Kellogg-Briand Pact Resigns from Post as President of the Hague Court Due to Circumstances Preventing Attendance

(Geneva) According to news today, former US Secretary of State Kellogg has resigned from his post as President of the International Court of Justice at The Hague because circumstances prevent him from attending the World Court. Kellogg is famous for initiating the Kellogg-Briand Pact, which was signed in Paris on August 27, 1928. In 1930, Kellogg was elected as a judge of the World Court. (Reuters, 23rd)

Current Status of the French Navy: Two Battleships Under Construction

(Paris) At a time when the world is paying attention to the military strength of various countries, a statement by Naval Minister Pietri to a reporter from "Le Journal" regarding the current state of the French Navy has attracted great attention. Pietri said that since the European War, no country has made as much effort to restore its navy as France. To date, France has a total of 426,000 tons of naval vessels available for deployment. This does not include the two 35,000-ton warships approved by the National Assembly. However, this is not an expansion of armaments. The tonnage of the French fleet is still one-third less than in 1914, as 140,000 tons were lost during the Great War, and efforts were not made to make up for the shortfall after 1915. Pietri also said that the main task at present is to build battleships, as France only has six old-style armored ships and three other old ships. However, this shortfall can be made up once the "Dunkerque," the "Strasbourg," and two other 35,000-ton ships are built. The construction of two 32,000-ton ships was approved at the beginning of this year. (National Press, 22nd)

Soviet Russia Reorganizes Army, Modeling After French Military System

(Moscow) The Central Executive Committee and the People's Committee of Soviet Russia have issued three orders to reorganize the Red Army, modeling it after the French military system. At the same time, a Red Army General Staff is being established, and the highest rank for officers is General, awarded exclusively to talented and outstanding officers and soldiers. Political circles explain that this new legislation means that the theory of equality has been abolished even in the Red Army. (National Telegram, 23rd)

(Moscow) People's Commissar for Defence of the Soviet Union, Voroshilov, issued the following instructions regarding the recent Red Army exercises in the Kiev Military District: "The Soviet Red Army of the Kiev Military District reflects the victorious development of various constructions and demonstrates the tremendous success of its various military trainings. The political and mental level of the troops participating in the exercises is extremely high." Voroshilov also stated that this war exercise extensively applied the latest military technical equipment and demonstrated the complete nature of modern warfare. He also pointed out that a large number of personnel jumping from airplanes, their organization, technology, and skills were outstanding, and their military actions during and after landing were also commendable. In his order, Voroshilov expressed his gratitude to the Commander of the Kiev Military District, his deputies, and all personnel participating in the exercises and ordered that the names of personnel with outstanding performance be submitted for recognition and reward. (TASS, 23rd)

(Moscow) The Soviet Central Executive Committee and the People's Committee promulgated an order to define the ranks of Red Army generals and stipulate the regulations for generals' service. It stated that the socialist construction in recent years has been largely victorious, and the Red Army has undergone long-term improvements in organization and technology, thus transforming into an advanced and first-class army. It possesses the latest military technology, and its command cadres are cultivated by the Communist Party, making them the most valuable asset. The Party has a slogan: "Cadres decide everything." This slogan, when applied to the Red Army, creates various conditions to ensure the continued growth and completion of the Red Army's cadres and commanders. Red Army commanders, such as commanders and political workers, are increasingly becoming lifelong careers. This career has its own characteristics, so service in this role must be clearly defined by law. All commanders must bear a special responsibility, namely, to train and cultivate Red Army talent. Commanders have a guiding role on the battlefield, so various ranks must be clearly defined. Then, each individual's military and special qualifications, past experiences, and their power and position in the Red Army can be clearly expressed.

"The Soviet Central Executive Committee and the People's Committee have decided that the Red Army commanders should be divided into the following command and special military ranks: Land and Air Force commanders are divided into Lieutenant, Captain, Major, Lieutenant Colonel, Colonel, Brigade Commander, Division Commander, Corps Commander, First-Class Army Commander, and Second-Class Army Commander. In the Navy, they are divided into Lieutenant, Captain Lieutenant, Captain, Lieutenant Commander, First-Class Captain, Second-Class Captain, First-Class Flag Officer, and Second-Class Flag Officer. Other troops will implement new ranks. In addition, a 'Soviet General' rank will be established, exclusively awarded by the Soviet Central Executive Committee to the highest-ranking officers with outstanding merits." The above resolution instructs to review all commanders and assign them ranks separately. Another directive from the Soviet People's Committee will rename the Red Army Staff Department as the Red Army General Staff. (TASS, 23rd)

US Army Chief of Staff Proposes Five-Year Military Expansion Plan

Add 800 Aircraft Annually; Army Strives for Motorization

(Washington) US Army Chief of Staff General MacArthur submitted his annual report to President Roosevelt today, advocating that 800 aircraft should be added annually over the next five years. MacArthur was recently appointed by Roosevelt as a military advisor to the Philippine Commonwealth government. This major proposal to expand the air force can be seen as his farewell gift to the US Army. MacArthur's report also stated that the Army, now that Congress is no longer obstructing, has entered a fiscal year of developing into a sufficient defense force and adapting to the minimum needs of the country, for the first time since 1922. MacArthur also outlined his five-year plan for the Army in the report as follows: (1) Replace all livestock-based operations with motorization; (2) Equip every infantryman with a new semi-automatic rifle, followed by the guards; (3) Modernize all field artillery; (4) Equip each army with anti-aircraft artillery; (5) Continue to experiment with chemical warfare tactics; (6) Gradually accumulate munitions. (National Telegram, 22nd)

Italy's Wartime Economic Resources; Solely Depend on Raising Bonds

(London) The "Financial News" published an article on Italy's economic resources in wartime, stating that "If a war breaks out, it goes without saying that the supply of various raw materials needed by the Italian army will face various difficulties due to economic sanctions. In addition, if the war lasts for several months, the gold reserves of the Italian National Bank will also be quickly exhausted. From this, it can be seen that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini intends for the war to end in a short period, even if a war breaks out. If so, although Italy's financial situation is quite depleted, it should not be difficult to raise public bonds domestically to finance military expenses. From past experience, countries can often rely on raising domestic debt to overcome difficulties during wartime and prevent financial bankruptcy. Although Italy has increased its domestic debt by a huge amount in recent years while peaceful, it can still be supported. Now, if a war breaks out, even if the domestic debt increases to an alarming amount, technically, it should not exceed the possible range." (Havas, 23rd)

Philippine Assembly Holds Final Session

Final Preparations for Commonwealth Government; Roosevelt Congratulates Quezon on Being Elected President

Manila: The Philippine Assembly held its final session today to make final preparations for the Commonwealth government. The Philippine Assembly is a bicameral system elected by the people of the Philippines, established under the Jones Law of 1916. After the establishment of the Commonwealth government, it will be changed to a unicameral system. The current Assembly will not discuss tariff issues, but the granting of operating rights to US airlines will be considered first to allow Pacific Aviation to start operations as soon as possible. The US Vice President, Secretary of War, and members of Congress will come to participate in the Commonwealth government's inauguration ceremony, and 50,000 yuan has been allocated for entertainment expenses. In addition, it will be decided to cede 15 or 20 acres of land in front of Manila Port to the United States for the establishment of offices and residences for US officials. (National Telegram, 23rd)

(Washington) President Roosevelt sent a telegram to Quezon, the newly elected first president of the Philippine Commonwealth government, today, sincerely congratulating him, saying, "Your Excellency's unanimous support from the majority of the people demonstrates Your Excellency's many years of hard work and great achievements for the country." Shandong Branch of the Chinese Cultural Construction Association Opposes Land Collectivization

Yan's Claims Violate Party Guidelines; Suggest Central Government Refrain From Discussion

Jinan Correspondence: Yan Xishan, the Pacification Commissioner of Shanxi, advocated for land collectivization, which has attracted much attention from the people of the country. Today (the 21st), the Shandong branch of the Chinese Cultural Construction Association held its third cadre meeting at the Department of Education. Cadre Li Tianni proposed an impromptu motion, stating that Yan Xishan's recently published advocacy of land collectivization is greatly contrary to the Three Principles of the People of the Premier [Sun Yat-sen]. He requested that the branch thoroughly study the matter, formulate a suggestion, and submit it to the general association, which would then forward it to the Fifth National Congress to suggest that this proposal not be discussed. He also entrusted Branch Director He to suggest, when attending the Fifth National Congress, that the proposal not be discussed. Cadre Wu Zicheng spoke, elaborating on and supplementing Li's proposal, asserting that Yan Xishan's advocacy is tantamount to opposing the Party and should be corrected. Chairman He Siyuan put it to discussion. Many cadres spoke, all agreeing that the Party's Principle of People's Livelihood already has clear regulations regarding restricting capital and equalizing land ownership. Yan Xishan, as a member of the Central Committee, should naturally be aware of this. Yet, he now has such an advocacy that violates the Party's political guidelines. Some who do not know the inside story even express sympathy with him. If it is turned over to the association for study, what is the difference between that land collectivization method and that of the Communist Party? Moreover, with land collectivization, the number of people in this village and that village is different, and the amount of land is also different. Disputes between villages will inevitably arise. This method is fundamentally unworkable and will only increase national disputes. At this time of multiple national crises, this heresy should be corrected, and so on. The chairman put it to a vote, and it was unanimously passed. It was resolved that Li Tianni and Liu Daoyuan would draft the document and submit it to the general association, which would then forward it to the Sixth Plenary Session of the Central Committee and the Fifth National Congress. The meeting then adjourned.

International Commercial Telegram

-Reuter's Special Business Report of September 23-

Gold and Silver: British Gold: The London gold price today was 141 shillings and 6 pence, up 10 pence.

British Silver: The London silver market was quiet today. Spot and futures were both 29 and 43125, up 0.0625 each. The United States bought, and China sold. The closing market was stable.

Exchange Rates: British-American: The London foreign exchange market was quiet this morning. Merchants are awaiting developments in the European situation. The opening exchange rate for British pounds against American dollars was 4.99 and 18125, which is 1875 higher than the closing price on Saturday. It fell 125 in the first hour, continued to fall 5625 at 1 PM, and fell another 0625 at 2 PM, to 4 dollars 910625.

Xiamen: Significant Tax Evasion on Sugar

Smugglers Are Organized and Armed; Customs Authorities Are Unable to Investigate

Xiamen Correspondence: In Xiamen, due to special circumstances, there are many operators who evade customs duties. Although customs authorities are making every effort to investigate and suppress them, these operators are organized, have backgrounds, and are a large-scale and well-funded group that has wide connections and unpredictable tactics. Although news of customs seizing smuggled goods is heard daily, only one out of ten is caught, and the losses are extremely minimal. Taking洋 sugar alone, Xiamen consumes at least 2,000 bags of sugar per month. However, according to customs statistics, from January 1st to September 19th of this year, only 4,969 bags of sugar were imported. These 4,969 bags of sugar were mostly transported to the Zhangzhou area for sale after import. In reality, not a single bag was imported into the city itself. Given that the city needs 2,000 bags of sugar per month and there is no local sugar production, it is all smuggled洋 sugar. This is an open secret in Xiamen, and people generally say, "Xiamen white sugar has no tax." According to reliable investigations, smuggled sugar arrives in Xiamen mostly from Qingyu and Gangwei outside Xiamen Port. It comes from the other side mostly loaded on large sailing ships or fishing boats. After reaching the destination, it is successively transported out using fishing boats, small sailing boats, and large double-oared boats. The transportation is disciplined, step-by-step, and has security. For example, when transporting by sailing ship or fishing boat, the one carrying the most cargo occupies a safe position and is supported by three other ships carrying less cargo. If they encounter a customs anti-smuggling ship, they will first use a ship with less cargo to deliberately create a panicked escape, attracting the attention of the customs ship. The other two ships will provide remote support. Even if one or two ships are caught, the loss is minimal. The heavily loaded ship has already landed on the other shore during this chaos. There must be bodyguards on this fully loaded ship, ranging from twenty to more than ten, all of whom are armed thugs. Whenever customs ships pursue these heavily loaded ships, they will inevitably open fire in resistance. The other three ships will also surround the customs ships. When customs ships encounter this, in the difficult situation of having to respond to the enemy, the fully loaded ship will set sail and fly away. The loading and unloading locations are Heshan, Wutong, and Fan Jiao on the Xiamen shore. This is in terms of Xiamen. In Quanzhou, it is on the coast outside Dongshi Port Nanmen. It is even more difficult for customs ships to fully investigate. In the Zhangzhou area, the situation was not as severe as in Xiamen and Quanzhou. The only income from sugar tax comes from this line. Recently, smuggled goods have also been pouring in from the seaport. Zhangpu has even more large-scale organizations, transporting and selling goods by car from Funan Bridge. Therefore, in August, Xiamen Customs transported 1,000 bags of sugar to the Zhangzhou area. This month, from the 1st to the 19th, there were only 100 bags in two weeks. These two places have become the main channels for the import of smuggled sugar into the Zhangzhou area. In summary, the huge loss of sugar tax revenue in the three places of Zhangzhou, Quanzhou, and Xiamen cannot be calculated. (September 21st)

Guangdong Province Restricts the Transportation of Silver Within the Country

Strictly Preventing Dishonest Merchants from Roundabout Export; Transportation of Silver Within the Province Requires a License

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since Guangdong Province banned the export of silver, the large-scale export of silver dollars has virtually disappeared. However, since Guangdong Province is located near the ocean, there are still a few dishonest merchants who transport silver dollars into inland ports under the pretext of entering the mainland, and then转运 them overseas in order to conceal their activities from the outside world. The authorities have already formulated measures for the transportation of silver within the country, stipulating that transportation is only permitted if the local port chamber of commerce issues a license. However, difficulties sometimes arise due to procedural issues. Recently, the Guangdong Department of Finance, in order to cope with this situation, specially formulated measures for the transportation of silver coins within the province and the procedures for obtaining licenses, which were approved by the Southwest Political Affairs Committee and circulated to the Guangdong Customs and Shantou and Hainan Customs for compliance. The measures are as follows: (1) If merchants in this province transport毛洋 coins or big dollar coins within the province to areas where毛洋 coins or big dollar coins have always been in circulation, the ships carrying them must pass through the ocean outside of the province and then re-enter the province, or if the transportation destination is on the national border, they can leave the country immediately after arrival. If transporters may export them overseas by way of circumventing the law, in addition to being allowed to carry a limited amount of ten yuan in accordance with the 銀禁条例, carrying anything more will be handled in accordance with the supplementary measures to crackdown on the smuggling of hard currency from the mainland via roundabout routes, and the provisions of these regulations. (2) These regulations do not apply to the transportation of silver coins within the province that does not involve the circumstances mentioned in the preceding paragraph. (3) For the transportation of silver coins within the province, if the circumstances mentioned in the preceding paragraph exist, a reputable firm with a business license must be found in Guangzhou to provide a guarantee in accordance with the supplementary measures, and the Department of Finance will specify the number of silver coins that are permitted to be transported and issue a transportation license. If the Department of Finance entrusts the Customs Supervisory Office or a Customs branch to issue transportation licenses on its behalf, the local procedures will continue to be followed. (4) When declaring imports and exports, the license must be presented to the customs for verification. After the customs have completed the verification, the date of verification and release must be written on the license and stamped with a seal before it is released. After the goods have been transported to the destination, the merchant must submit the license to the original issuing agency for cancellation within the prescribed time limit. (5) Whether exporting or importing silver coins, merchants must be limited to locations where customs offices are established. Whether the silver coins are transported by ferry, they must be listed on the ferry's manifest and declared to customs for verification. (6) Regardless of which agency issues the transportation license, the Department of Finance may at any time secretly order officials of the relevant local agency to investigate whether a merchant has transported silver coins to that location and sold them abroad to profit from smuggling. If such circumstances exist, even if the original license has been canceled, the guarantor firm and the declaring merchant cannot be relieved of their responsibility. (7) Wuzhou is an inland commercial port outside this province, but the commercial relationship between this province and Wuzhou is close. These regulations specifically treat Wuzhou as the same as inland areas of this province. However, since the commercial relationship between Wuzhou and Guangzhou is in a position of import excess over exports, if a merchant transports silver from Guangzhou to Wuzhou, the reason for the need to transport silver should be reported in detail to the Department for approval before a license can be issued. (September 16th)

Completion of Huainan Railway

Planning to Build Yuxikou Terminal Station; Joint Operations with Jiangnan Railway

Wuhu Correspondence: The Huainan Railway, built by the Huainan Coal Mining Bureau, starts from Tianjia'an, the location of the coal mine, and passes through Datong, Huaian, Shuijiahu, Zhuxiang, Xiatangji, Luoji, Shuangdunji, Hefei, Cuozhen, Qiaotouji, Jiongjiang River, Zhonggan, and finally Yuxikou on the opposite bank of Wuhu, with a total length of more than 180 kilometers. Since construction began, the project has progressed rapidly. The section from Tianjia'an to the county seat of Chaoxian was completed and opened to traffic at the end of last month, transporting coal and attaching fourth-class passenger cars. It has been operating for two weeks, and business is quite prosperous. As for the section from Chaoxian to Yuxikou on the opposite bank of Wuhu, the final destination, it is about 60 kilometers long. The earthwork for the roadbed has now been completely built. However, because there are more than 30 bridges, the project is more difficult and will take longer. As soon as it is completed within the deadline, track laying will begin. Yesterday, a person in charge of the road came to Wuhu from the mine to discuss matters with the Wuhu Jiangnan Railway Company. According to the conversation, Yuxi is the terminal station of the road and must operate jointly with the Wuhu Jiangnan Railway. Regarding the station foundation earthwork, the land has now been purchased and the construction is being planned. It is expected that all projects will be completed by the end of this year, and the entire line will begin operation. Passenger cars will be added in early March of next year to officially transport passengers. In order to facilitate the travel of merchants, joint operations will be carried out with the Jiangnan Railway. Wuhu to Yuxikou is a total of 25 Chinese miles. It is planned to purchase ferries to transport trains, similar to the Shanghai-Pinghu traffic plan, which can arrive in just half an hour. He went on to say that this light railway is extremely economical to build, costing less than other roads. After completion in the future, the transportation of Huainan coal will be convenient, and its sales will definitely be prosperous. Currently, coal from the mine is being transported to Chaoxian and then loaded onto civilian boats and towed to Wuhu by small轮ships for sale to various places upstream and downstream. In addition, according to Zhou Xiansong, the manager of the Jiangnan Railway Company, the surveying project for the expansion of the line from Sunjiabu has now reached the Hulesi Town area of Ningguo County. As soon as funds are raised, construction will begin. After reaching Tunxi in the future, Huangshan will inevitably become more prosperous. As for the Wuhu-Sunjiabu line, business has recently become increasingly prosperous. In order to facilitate the travel of passengers, after the newly purchased locomotives are transported to Wuhu, the number of trains will be increased from three to four per day, for a total of eight round trips. (21st)

Changzhou: Rickshaw Dispute Still Needs Reconsideration

The dispute between rickshaw owners and rickshaw drivers in Wujin County has lasted for a long time and has not yet been resolved in a fair manner. On the afternoon of the 16th of this month, Public Security Bureau Chief Xu Baoguang and First District Chief Lin Jun met with representatives of both labor and capital from the rickshaw industry to discuss a solution to the rent issue. As a result, the capital party must ensure that the rickshaw body and all equipment are in perfect condition and must be inspected by the county government on a regular basis. The rent should still be calculated at 30 cents of silver dollar in accordance with the order from the Province. Both parties unanimously agreed on the spot, and Bureau Chief Xu and District Chief Lin reported to the county government for approval. Subsequently, some rickshaw drivers rose up and declared that they had not sent representatives to participate in the discussions, denied the agreement, and jointly petitioned the county party headquarters for assistance. Currently, the county party headquarters, in order to avoid disputes, strongly advocates that both management and labor should adhere to the principle of coexistence and co-prosperity in order to seek a balanced solution. On the 22nd, a letter was sent to the county government convening a party-government talk session for reconsideration.

The Nantong County Government convened a meeting of district chiefs and decided to hold a week-long campaign to investigate opium and drugs at the beginning of next month. During this period, all military, police, and Baojia personnel in the county must be mobilized as a whole to investigate and suppress opium and drugs separately, aiming to achieve the goal of completely eliminating drugs. The entire county will be divided into five investigation areas, with an investigation committee and temporary shelter set up in each area. Hangzhou: Jiangpu Highway Transportation Strike

The Jiang (Shan) Pu (Cheng) highway on the border of Zhejiang and Fujian provinces has always relied heavily on the transportation of goods from Fujian province, with annual revenues of approximately 400,000 to 500,000 yuan. Recently, the Fujian Provincial Government, in order to improve the Yanpu, Yansha Yong, and Jianshao Guang highway projects, has specially allocated highway stock bonds based on the volume of exported goods: 10 cents per case of kerosene, 5.5 cents per case of soap, 2.5 yuan per 100 kilograms of native cloth, and the same for yarn, wool, cotton textiles, and leather products. A general office has been established in Pucheng to begin allocating the bonds. Merchants believe that the burden is equivalent to doubling the freight rate and have all gone on strike to show their resistance. It has been a week and has not yet been resolved. Chen Ticheng, the director of the Fujian Construction Department, came to Hangzhou yesterday to visit Zhu Yaoting, the director of the Highway Bureau, to discuss the matter.

Shaanxi-Chengdu Line to Open Tomorrow: New Aircraft Flew to Chengdu Yesterday

Arrived at Yan'an, then Bad Weather - Overnight Stay in Xi'an, Continuing Flight This Morning

Eurasia Aviation Corporation. After the new aircraft No. 52, ordered from German Lufthansa, arrived in Shanghai, it took off from Longhua Airport at 6:45 yesterday morning. Huang Runshu, director of the Shanghai County Public Funds and Property Office, and others sent a telegram to the Jiangsu Provincial Government requesting that officials be sent to survey the famine in Shanghai County: "To the Provincial Government, Civil Affairs Department, and Finance Department: This year, from the spring and summer equinoxes, the weather was extremely dry, and the sowing of cotton and rice was already delayed. Fortunately, after the summer, the rainfall was well-distributed, and the growth was quite lush. Unexpectedly, after the autumn equinox, the rain continued, coupled with the intense heat, most of the cotton bolls that had formed rotted, and those that had not formed were lost. The rice ears were just at the time of grain formation when they were suddenly devastated by wind and rain, drooping and collapsing, mostly showing white ears. In addition, with continuous flooding for days, most of them germinated, withered, and fell off, all of which are visible to the eye. It is now estimated that the harvest loss is quite large. The farmers' hard work throughout the year has suddenly been hit by a disaster, and they are extremely distressed. The rural areas have been on the verge of collapse for years, and with another poor harvest, what future troubles can be imagined? Witnessing the situation, it is difficult to remain silent. Therefore, we are sending a special telegram to request your office to quickly send officials to the countryside for inspection and to plan for compassion. We will not dare to be negligent. Lu Bohong's Letter Reports the Process of Visiting the Disaster Area in Shandong

Three Million Disaster Victims in More Than Ten Counties in the Disaster Area - Relief Funds Distributed, Half for Shelter and Half for Emergency Relief

The General Association for the Relief of Flood Victims in Various Provinces received a letter from Lu Bohong, the director of the inspection and relief efforts in Shandong Province, reporting on the process of visiting the disaster area in Shandong. The original letter is summarized below: "I departed from Shanghai on the afternoon of the 17th and arrived in Jinan on the evening of the 18th. I visited various disaster victim shelters. Jinan City has sheltered more than 20,000 disaster victims, divided into 27 shelters. I visited the 9th, 13th, 16th, 17th, and 18th shelters until 11:00 PM. I had discussions with the leaders of the Shandong Provincial Party and government on everything. Currently, the disaster area in western Shandong covers more than ten counties, with no fewer than three million disaster victims. About 300,000 people have been sheltered in various counties, so rescuing those who have not escaped is especially urgent. The allocation of funds is planned to use half to supplement the various shelter organizations and half to handle emergency relief in the disaster area. The Shandong Relief Association and the Public Education Progress Association will cooperate in distributing relief funds. It is now planned to establish an office in Jining. Please send clothing and other items for relief to Yanzhou, which has convenient transportation with Jinan and Jining. In Jinan shelters, women and children account for the majority, and there are records of children falling ill and dying. It is requested to establish medical institutions, and the mayor has strongly requested this. It has been decided to set up two temporary hospitals in Jinan. After I return to Shanghai, male and female doctors and dozens of female nurses will be sent. Caozhou, Jining, and other places will also need hospitals. I will report again after future inspections. I can return to Shanghai around the 25th to report in person. The Shandong relief funds should be remitted gradually after I return to Shanghai. I am now requesting Shandong Bishop Yang, Caozhou Priest Wan, and Yanggu Bishop Tian to help with the distribution of relief to avoid wasting the relief funds."

Swire's Regular Northern Route Liner Yuezhou Suffers Engine Damage

Haikou Ship Sent to Tow Back to Shanghai - Must Enter Dock for Major Repairs

The Swire Company's new ship Yuezhou, on its regular northern route, is the sister ship of the new Shuntian ship in terms of size and style, both operating on the North China route. Since arriving in Shanghai, this is the 23rd time it has sailed outwards, including this export trip. The ship was fully loaded with outbound cargo destined for Qingdao, Yantai, Tianjin and other ports for unloading. Because of its speed, the ship is very popular with passengers traveling north. Shanghai to Qingdao takes only 24 hours.

Mid-Trip Engine Damage. Initially, the voyage from Shanghai was quite smooth, but around dusk on the 20th, as it was approaching the outside of Qingdao port, the ship's engine suddenly broke down and the ship lost its ability to navigate, failing to enter Qingdao port. The shipowner telegraphed the Qingdao branch, which immediately dispatched a small steamship from Qingdao to attempt to tow the ship into Qingdao port to unload cargo and passengers.

Ship Sent to Replace. The Shanghai company received the telegram and immediately ordered the company's Hunan ship to transport the cargo and passengers of the Yuezhou ship to Yantai and Tianjin for unloading.

Tow to Shanghai for Major Repairs. Yesterday afternoon, the Shanghai office had already decided that the company's Haikou ship, which was transporting cargo south from Tianjin, would be telegraphed to Qingdao to tow the damaged Yuezhou ship back to Shanghai. According to reliable information from the company, the ship is expected to enter port around the afternoon of tomorrow (the 25th). After arriving in Shanghai, engineers must first inspect the extent of the engine damage before it can enter the dock for major repairs.

Municipal Federation Sends Letter to Municipal Chamber of Commerce Urging Response to Rent Reduction Movement

The Municipal Federation of Citizens of the First Special District sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday: "Dear Sirs, Since the outbreak of the Shanghai War, the vitality of the market in this city has been greatly damaged, and industry and commerce are exhausted to the extreme. The phenomenon of shops being unable to sustain themselves and declaring bankruptcy has become widespread. There are many reasons for this unfortunate situation, but the high cost of rent is also a major factor. However, most landlords are greedy and disregard the rent reduction movement, even relying on the law to oppress tenants, so that Shanghai, which is known as prosperous, has suddenly become a scene of desolation. Our Federation deeply knows that to revitalize the market, rent reduction must come first. Therefore, we are determined to make thorough efforts. Our organization believes that your chamber of commerce is the leader of the Shanghai commercial group, and you have a close relationship with the rise and fall of industry and commerce and the welfare of the citizens in this city. When our association gathers the strength of all citizens to promote the realization of rent reduction and urges Chairman Chiang to issue rent reduction standards, your chamber of commerce should understand that reducing rent will solve the entire social and economic problem, and come forward to respond, so as to relieve the merchants of the city from upside down and pull millions of citizens out of the water and fire. We eagerly await your reply."

Seaport Quarantine Station Announced Yesterday: All Imported Used Goods Must Be Disinfected - Otherwise, Extraction Will Not Be Allowed, and the Station Will Handle Disinfection Procedures

The Shenshi News Agency reported that the Seaport Quarantine Administration has now stipulated that all imported used sacks, used cloth, used cotton wadding, used cotton yarn, used clothing, used pillowcases, waste wool, and used paper, etc., must be submitted with a disinfection certificate issued by the health authority of the country of origin upon import. If the certificate cannot be submitted, extraction will not be allowed unless the quarantine officials of the Administration conduct disinfection procedures. At the same time, all disinfection costs must be paid by the original importing merchant. This regulation will be implemented three months from the date of announcement.

Representatives of Banking and Money Industries Return to Shanghai to Discuss the Problem of Exemption from Stamp Duty on Checks

Wang Zhixin and Xi Jimin, the two representatives of the banking and money industries in this city, who were delegated to Nanjing to petition the Legislative Yuan for amendments regarding the stamp duty on checks, returned to Shanghai the night before. Yesterday morning, according to Mr. Wang, who spoke to a reporter from the Central News Agency, he met with Mr. Ma Yinchu, Chairman of the Finance Committee of the Legislative Yuan, in Nanjing and presented his views. The so-called two cents stamp duty on checks is a very small burden for the people, and the government's revenue is also small, but the procedures are very cumbersome, and the promotion of negotiable instruments in our country is not widespread, and the banking business is not very developed. If we want to develop China's economy, the government should actively assist. The issue of stamp duty, although small, is closely related to the development of the negotiable instruments system, and it is hoped that it can be revised. Mr. Ma expressed his acceptance of this idea and agreed to submit it to the meeting for reconsideration. The two representatives were satisfied and returned to Shanghai the night before to report back to the two associations. It is heard that the Stamp Tax Law is related to industry, commerce, finance and other industries. When the new law is promulgated, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce also believes that there are places that should be amended. The association is now soliciting opinions from various industries and drafting memoranda to submit to the Legislative Yuan. The insurance and shipping associations also have opinions to put forward. The Legislative Yuan will wait until the memoranda from various industries are submitted to the meeting before discussing them together.

Ministry of Finance Reply: Work Contracts Exempt from Stamp Duty, Not Within the Scope of Employment Contracts

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce previously received an inquiry from the Dachung Dong Match Company regarding how to affix stamps to labor employment contracts. The Chamber of Commerce verified that according to item 25 of the Stamp Tax Law rate schedule, except for appointment letters issued by government agencies and schools that are exempt, all other employment contracts require a stamp of two cents. However, ordinary employment contracts are issued by the employer or hiring party to the employed individual. The work contracts of the Dachung Hua Match Company's laborers, although held by both the employer and the worker, are actually documents established by the worker's side. This differs from the situation of employment contracts. In accordance with principle 4 of the Stamp Tax Law principles set by the Central Political Council, which aims to support farmers and workers, there was some doubt as to whether these contracts could be exempted from stamps. After reporting this to the Ministry of Finance via telegram, the Ministry of Finance issued reply No. 785, stating: "We have received and understood your telegram. Upon review, Article 16 and rate schedule item 25 of the Stamp Tax Law regarding employment contracts refer to documents for employing personnel to assume work. Upon examination of the work contracts for laborers used by the Dachung Hua Match Company, they are specifically for employing laborers and differ from employment contracts. Therefore, they are not within the scope of employment contracts. You should immediately inform them of this decision."

Astronomical Physics and Other Academic Societies: Preparing to Organize a Solar Eclipse Observation Team

Total Solar Eclipse Will Occur on June 19th Next Year. Two Teams Will be Formed, Budgeted at 150,000 Yuan

The Chinese Astronomical Society, the Chinese Physical Society, Academia Sinica, the Peiping Research Institute, the Tsingtao Observatory, the Zhongshan University Observatory, Zhu Kezhen, Li Shuhua of the Tsinghua University Graduate School, and others believe that the total solar eclipse on June 19th next year, which will be visible on the Sino-Russian border, is a rare opportunity in centuries. For the purpose of conducting field research, they have initiated the organization of a solar eclipse observation team composed of various academic groups. It is planned to divide the team into two groups, one going to Japan and the other to Russia. The estimated travel expenses and observation equipment costs are approximately 150,000 yuan. In addition to the 100,000 yuan raised by participating groups, they are also requesting subsidies from the central government. It is reported that countries around the world, such as Japan, Russia, Britain, and Germany, also have large-scale organizations engaged in observation, because after this period, it will not be discovered in central China again until 30 years later.

An Overview of Municipal Public Works Construction in the Past Year

Since the municipal authorities determined the Great Shanghai plan, the authorities have spared no effort in the construction of municipal public works. In the spring of this year, the municipal government dispatched Shen Yi, the director of the Public Works Bureau, to Europe and the West for inspection. Since Director Shen returned to China, he has carefully planned and strived to improve. The reporter has learned from the bureau the following overview of public works construction in the past year.

Central Urban Area: After the opening of the free central area, various buildings have been constructed one after another. Because the terrain in this area is relatively low, construction must first fill the soil. Therefore, the soil filling project is very large, estimated at more than 10,000 cubic meters. The second concession land and municipal government staff land total more than 1,000 acres, which can accommodate a total ditch of 30 to 90 cm, totaling more than 17,000 meters in length. In terms of road access, in addition to the newly opened Zhengjun East Road, the remaining roads have been gradually improved in order to achieve perfection. For example, Shiguang Road, Shixing Road, Minbei Road, and Minfu Road have all been successively repaved with cinder and gravel surfaces. As for Xiangyin Road from Shuidaidian Road to the central district branch of the Public Security Bureau, the original asphalt road surface was between 4 and 6 meters wide, and it had been severely damaged due to years of disrepair. The road surface has been widened to 9 meters with cold asphalt, and cement curbs have been built on the sides to tidy up the sidewalks. The road surface is smooth and wide, and it has been completely renewed. In terms of all public buildings, in addition to the sports field, swimming pool, gymnasium, and primary school projects, which have all been completed, the library, museum, municipal college, etc. will also be completed one after another soon.

Zhabei Area: Zhabei was severely damaged after the January 28th Incident. In recent years, it has been extensively renovated. For example, Hongjiang Road, Baoxing Road, Hongxing Road, Maichang Road, and Dongbaochang Road have all been rebuilt with asphalt road surfaces after being lighted, totaling more than 5,000 meters in length, and double curbs and cement sidewalks have been built. More than 1,000 meters of main ditches have been installed at Dongbaoshan Road and Jiaotong Road. Zhenda Road, Tonghe Road, Huasheng Road, etc., have more than 4,000 meters of cinder roads constructed. Jiangwan Wanshi Street, etc., have also been rebuilt with stone road surfaces. After the central part of the Zhabei district, since Baoshan Road and Qiujiang Road have been renovated and completed, the vertical and horizontal traffic has been greatly facilitated.

South Shanghai Area: In the South Shanghai area, Fangxie Road has low-lying terrain and no ditch facilities, and the road surface has been particularly damaged. Ditches and pipes have been constructed, the roadbed has been raised, and cold asphalt roads have been paved, covering 1,000 meters. Zhonghua Road originally had a stone road surface, and the trams running on it were particularly damaged. 1,800 meters of cold asphalt road surface were rebuilt. The Limar Road was originally a stone road surface, and the section near Dongmen was narrow and the traffic was heavy, which urgently needed to be improved. The section from Dongmen Road to the Dama Pier has been widened according to the prescribed route, and 500 meters of cold asphalt road surface have been rebuilt. Lujiabang Road was originally a cinder road surface, but as the city became more prosperous, the section east of Chezhan Road was paved with a stone road surface, 1,500 meters long, and the section west of Chezhan Road was paved with an asphalt road surface, 700 meters long. In addition, 500 feet of stone road surface were built on the Pubin Road.

Pudong Area: There were no heavy engineering projects in the Pudong area during the year, and most of them were improvements. For example, Chunshan Road was paved with stones and ditches were laid for more than 500 meters, Handu Road was paved with stones for more than 1,500 meters, Xiliqiao Road was paved with stones for more than 500 meters, and Zhanglou West Road and Lao Baitu were also successively rebuilt with stone road surfaces.

Yesterday morning, Mary's sister also specially accompanied Mary to An's residence to mediate between the two, hoping that both parties would reconcile. However, Mary and An had another conflict over a word, and even started fighting. An was momentarily angry, forgetting the old love of the past. Under the force of the moment, he actually broke Mary's right arm, causing her to fall to the ground in pain and writhe in pain. At this time, Anderson, seeing that he had caused trouble and recalling the past, suddenly felt pity again. He automatically reported to the police station, dispatched a car to send Mary to the Fumin Hospital on North Sichuan Road for treatment, and stated the process, deeply regretting his rashness. The Cihang Weekly newspaper office on the second floor of Juelin Vegetarian Restaurant, No. 254 Avenue Joffre, published news on June 17 this year about the replacement of abbots at the Li'an Temple in Hangzhou. The text involved damage to the reputation of the Hangzhou Buddhist Association. Therefore, Quefei (abbot of Lingyin Temple), Yuetao (abbot of Fajing Temple), and Benlian (abbot of Zhaoqing Temple), as standing committee members of the association and legal representatives, hired lawyer Gu Kenfu to file a lawsuit with the Criminal Court of the Second Branch, suing Zhong Lida, Liu Wuxi, and Long Jianxing, the issuing manager and editors of Cihang Weekly, for defamation, requesting legal investigation and prosecution, and attaching a civil lawsuit, requesting a judgment ordering the publication of the judgment in major Shanghai and Hangzhou newspapers for three days, and compensation for damages of one yuan. The case has been repeatedly subpoenaed by the First Special Court. Because the defendants did not arrive, the date was changed. This newspaper has already recorded the details. Yesterday, Judge Chen Pusheng of the Second Special Court held a hearing to continue the interrogation. None of the parties involved were present. Only the plaintiff's lawyer, Gu Kenfu, arrived and said that the case is currently being mediated and reconciled by layman Qu Yingguang and Wang Yiting, and they are currently in contact. He requested the court to allow the date to be changed again. He also said that the defendant had previously stated in court that Quefei had a relationship with his fourth concubine. Upon investigation, it was actually Gu Lutao who impersonated a reporter from the Weifeng News Agency and published in the newspaper that Quefei had an affair with a certain nun. After Quefei saw the report, he also published a statement to defend himself. After Chen Xiaopu, the president of the Weifeng News Agency, learned about it, he investigated and prosecuted Gu Lutao in the Hangzhou Local Court. As a result, Gu was sentenced to three months in prison for two crimes of intimidation. Case file No. 93 of the 18th year can be checked. It is sufficient to show that the facts stated by the defendant are also inconsistent and deliberately defame the reputation, etc. After verifying the words, the court approved the change of date to 10:00 AM on the 30th of this month for another interrogation.

Bao Yongsheng, a native of Ningbo, is 20 years old and works as a student at a certain electrical materials company on Zhapu Road. Through Train Tickets for Two Roads and Zhenyang Long-Distance Buses: Price Changes, Effective October 1st

The Lianglu Administration has now approved a letter from the Zhenyang Long-Distance Bus Company stating that from October 1st of this year, the one-way bus fare between Zhenjiang and Yangzhou will be 80 cents per passenger, regardless of class. Round-trip first class will cost 1.20 yuan per passenger, and third class will cost 1.36 yuan per passenger. In addition, the one-way fare between Zhenjiang and Shijiaqiao will be 40 cents per passenger, regardless of class. The transfer fee between the station and the company's pier will be 20 cents per passenger one way and 40 cents round trip, which will be collected as usual. The implementation will start from October 1st. Please instruct the stations to transport according to the instructions. In addition to asking the accounting office to correct the price when adding new tickets, each station will sell old tickets from that day and change the price to be unused in red pen first.

The Executive Yuan Issues a Circular to All Provinces and Cities to Suspend Slaughter for One Day

October 4th is World Animal Day. The China Animal Protection Society will follow the procedures of last year's commemorative meeting and hold the second publicity meeting on this day at the City Chamber of Commerce. A membership recruitment meeting will also be held at the same time. In addition, a request has been submitted to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Interior to issue a circular to all provinces, cities, and counties across the country to suspend slaughter for one day. The details are recorded as follows:

Publicity Meeting World Animal Day on October 4th originated in the United States and has been around for over a hundred years. This year is the 101st anniversary. Major commemorative events are held in various European and American countries. The Shanghai Animal Protection Society initiated a publicity meeting last year. With this year's Animal Day approaching, the society will follow last year's commemorative procedures and hold the second publicity meeting at the City Chamber of Commerce in Tianhou Palace at 1:00 PM this afternoon. A membership recruitment meeting will also be held at the same time to promote the cause.

(7) Negotiate with various cinemas to add promotional films on this day, which will be handled by Yang Shuchu. (8) The conference will invite celebrities to take turns giving speeches. (9) Submit a request to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Interior to issue a circular to all provinces, cities, and counties across the country to suspend slaughter for one day in order to show the ultimate intention of protecting animals.

Suspend Slaughter for One Day Ye Gongchuo, the chairman of the association, stated that for World Animal Day on October 4th, the Executive Yuan had been requested to issue a circular to all countries to exempt all kinds of animals from slaughter for one day. The Executive Yuan has already instructed the Ministry of Interior to instruct all levels of government across the country to comply with the re-election of Zhao Jinqing and other directors.

Two Cases of Smuggling Silver for Export Sentenced Separately

Liu Maolan, a food steward on the Dalian Maru transport ship, smuggled 1,210 dimes in small silver coins on the 22nd of last month, intending to take them to Dalian for profit. Before the ship weighed anchor, he was found by customs officers for violating the Provisional Regulations on Prohibiting the Export of Silver Coins promulgated by the National Government of the Republic of China on July 15, 24. Therefore, Liu Maolan was immediately arrested and sent to the local court for trial. In addition, a foreign national, Huang Jingyuan, attempted to smuggle 54 silver coins, and was also caught by customs officers. He was sent to the court for interrogation and prosecution separately in the criminal court. After the debate ended, Judge He held a court session yesterday afternoon and announced the sentence. He ordered Liu Maolan and others to be brought to the case, and after a brief interrogation, he stood up and announced the sentence: Liu Maolan's case of obstructing national currency (main text): Liu Maolan attempted to smuggle coins for profit and failed. He was sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment, and the 1,210 silver coins smuggled for export were confiscated. Huang Jingyuan was sentenced to two years of imprisonment, and the 54 silver coins smuggled were confiscated. After the sentence, they were returned to custody to await the expiration of the appeal period before being sent to prison for execution.

The civil lawsuit's three-month term has expired, and the criminal lawsuit was also acquitted

Ye was in room No. 3 of the detention center. Criminal Court Judge Chen Pusheng held a court session with Prosecutor Wang on the morning of the 19th to hear the case and announced the conclusion. He scheduled a date for sentencing, which has been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday was the date for sentencing. After the court filed the report, it immediately commissioned Prosecutor Tang Ruxiu to lead the forensic examiners to the scene. It was found that the corpse was approximately thirty years old, wearing a blue coarse cloth short shirt, ant cloth pants, white thread socks, and black shoes, resembling a worker. The corpse had severe injuries to the throat, and both the trachea and esophagus were severed, which was the cause of death. After filling out the forms and taking photos, because no family members came forward to identify the body, it was instructed to have the funeral home provide a coffin and shroud. Because there was no blood on the corpse's side of the field and nearby, it seemed that the body was thrown there after being murdered. The police station in charge has ordered detectives to conduct a secret investigation.

Gave Birth Seven Months After Marriage

The Child Was Found to Belong to the Brother-in-Law, Not Constituting an Offense Against Public Morality

Pan Xiaomei, a woman from Jiangyin, is eighteen years old. She lost her mother at a young age and has been living in her brother-in-law Zhou Bingrong's house at No. 6 Ping'an Lane, Yangjiazhai, Pudong, for the past few years. It is said that she married Ji Shiming, a blacksmith from the same town, at No. 45 Lane 35, Yangjiazhai, on the sixteenth day of the twelfth month of the lunar calendar. However, she gave birth to a baby girl just seven months after marriage. Ji knew that something was wrong because the child was not yet a full term. Li was furious and sent the baby girl to Zhou's house yesterday morning, but Zhou refused to accept it, resulting in a dispute. The police arrived at the scene and took the plaintiff Ji Shiming, the defendant Zhou Bingrong, and Xiaomei to the Pudong Branch Bureau. According to Ji's statement, his wife was raped before marriage, resulting in the pregnancy. He requested an investigation. According to Xiaomei's confession, it was true that she had been raped by her brother-in-law once. According to Zhou's statement, Xiaomei had been in his house for three years, and in the second half of last year, he had a physical relationship with her. After she became pregnant, she married Ji. Ji and his father-in-law knew about this beforehand, and both parties were willing. Now Li is using this to blackmail him, asking to borrow fifty yuan in silver unsuccessfully, and suddenly sent the child, causing a dispute. Director Zhang investigated and found that the case involved the rape of a woman under the age of twenty, and the pregnancy was followed by a marriage, which was an offense against public morality. He ordered that both the plaintiff and defendant be sent to the headquarters for interrogation.

Two Corpses, Blood Staining the Ground

Mrs. Jin Was Already Dead; The Maid Was Barely Alive. Photography Studio Employee Pushed the Door Open and Shouted in Horror

The address at No. 459, the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and North Henan Road, is an old Western-style single-family house. The lessee is a Suzhou widow in her forties, with a son and a daughter aged about fifteen or sixteen. Her son is studying at the Public School in the Northern District of the Shanghai Municipal Council on Ke Neng Hai Road. People generally call the woman Mrs. Jin. Her second floor and the bottom floor are rented to Rong Kang Hua Xing and Xie Long Trading Company. She lives on the third floor, and only hires a maid to serve her. Her daily life seems to be that of a petty bourgeois family. At about 10:00 AM yesterday morning, when Mrs. Jin had not yet gotten up, a photography studio assigned an employee to deliver photos taken by Mrs. Jin some time ago. At that time, the employee saw that Mrs. Jin's door was closed, so he knocked on the door and called out. However, there was no response for a long time, so he pushed the door open, and the door was not locked. To his surprise, there were two corpses in front of his eyes. After careful examination, one was Mrs. Jin and the other was the maid. Blood stained the ground. At that time, the employee was horrified and shouted, quickly turned around and went downstairs, and rushed to the Huishi Police Station to report. After receiving the report, the police station immediately dispatched detectives to investigate and found that Mrs. Jin had already died, and the maid was dying, covered in knife wounds. They quickly sent the maid to the Sanatorium Hospital for treatment, and sent Mrs. Jin's body to the morgue for autopsy, and carefully examined the remains in the room and took pictures for filing. As for the reason for the murder, there are different opinions. If the maid can be saved, the case will not be difficult to solve.
